CREATE TABLE odi_Cap(
   Name        VARCHAR(24) NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY
  ,Year        VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL
  ,Played      INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Won         INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Lost        INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Tied        INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,"No result" INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Win         INTEGER  NOT NULL
);

CREATE TABLE odi_Player(
   id    INTEGER  NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY 
  ,Name  VARCHAR(33) NOT NULL
  ,First INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Last  INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Mat   INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Inn   INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,NO    INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Run   INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,HS    VARCHAR(4) NOT NULL
  ,Avg   NUMERIC(5,2) NOT NULL
  ,Balls INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Mdn   INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Runs  INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Wkt   INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,BBM   VARCHAR(6) NOT NULL
  ,Avgs  NUMERIC(6,2) NOT NULL
  ,Ca    INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,St    INTEGER  NOT NULL
);

CREATE TABLE Test_Cap(
   Name   VARCHAR(24) NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY
  ,Year   VARCHAR(12) NOT NULL
  ,Played INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Won    INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Lost   INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Tied   INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Win    NUMERIC(5,2) NOT NULL
);

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS Test_player;
CREATE TABLE Test_player(
   Cap          VARCHAR(6) NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY
  ,Name         VARCHAR(27) NOT NULL
  ,First        INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Last         INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Mat          VARCHAR(6) NOT NULL
  ,Runs         VARCHAR(5) NOT NULL
  ,HS           VARCHAR(4) NOT NULL
  ,Avg          VARCHAR(5) NOT NULL
  ,Wkt          VARCHAR(3) NOT NULL
  ,BBI          VARCHAR(6) NOT NULL
  ,Ave          VARCHAR(6) NOT NULL
  ,"510 wicket" VARCHAR(9) NOT NULL
  ,Ca           INTEGER 
  ,St           INTEGER 
);

SELECT * FROM test_player;
SELECT * FROM odi_player;

CREATE TABLE Match(
   Match_Id            INTEGER  NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY 
  ,Match_Date          VARCHAR(9) NOT NULL
  ,Team_Name_Id        INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Opponent_Team_Id    INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Season_Id           INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Venue_Name          VARCHAR(52) NOT NULL
  ,Toss_Winner_Id      INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Toss_Decision       VARCHAR(5) NOT NULL
  ,IS_Superover        INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,IS_Result           INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Is_DuckWorthLewis   INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Win_Type            VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL
  ,Won_By              INTEGER 
  ,Match_Winner_Id     INTEGER 
  ,Man_Of_The_Match_Id INTEGER 
  ,First_Umpire_Id     INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Second_Umpire_Id    INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,City_Name           VARCHAR(14) NOT NULL
  ,Host_Country        VARCHAR(12) NOT NULL
);

CREATE TABLE Player(
   Player_Id     INTEGER  NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY 
  ,Player_Name   VARCHAR(21) NOT NULL
  ,DOB           VARCHAR(9)
  ,Batting_Hand  VARCHAR(10)
  ,Bowling_Skill VARCHAR(22)
  ,Country       VARCHAR(12) NOT NULL
  ,Is_Umpire     INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,FIELD8        INTEGER 
);

SELECT * FROM ODI_Career ;

CREATE TABLE ODI_Career(
   Player  VARCHAR(16) NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY
  ,Debut   INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Last    INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Matches INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,Runs    INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,HS      VARCHAR(4) NOT NULL
  ,BatAvg  NUMERIC(5,2) NOT NULL
  ,"100 C" INTEGER 
  ,Wkts    INTEGER 
  ,BowAvg  NUMERIC(6,2)
  ,"5 W"   INTEGER 
  ,Catches INTEGER  NOT NULL

CREATE TABLE T20_Century(
   Id   INTEGER NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY
  ,Player     VARCHAR(15) NOT NULL
  ,Runs       VARCHAR(4) NOT NULL
  ,Balls      INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,"4 S"      INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,"6 S"      INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,SR         NUMERIC(6,2) NOT NULL
  ,Team       VARCHAR(5) NOT NULL
  ,Opposition VARCHAR(14) NOT NULL
  ,Ground     VARCHAR(15) NOT NULL
);
